## Coverage grid inspection

- Geography: OSM `addr:city` values and coordinate-only records span the saved isochrone; targeted rows cover central, east, west, south, north, and mobile/catchment-wide formats.
- Language/script: English/Latin dominates public listings; Spanish searches ran; non-ASCII/local-name rows are flagged in structured data.
- Cuisine/tradition: broad OSM cuisine tags plus targeted Mexican, Oaxacan, Veracruz, Chinese, Taiwanese, Japanese, Ethiopian/Oromo, Somali, Swahili, Afghan, Nepalese, Georgian, Peruvian, Colombian, Venezuelan, Sicilian, and other regional searches were inspected.
- Service format: restaurant, cafe, fast food, pub/bar-with-food candidates, takeaway, counter, food truck/pop-up, caterer/private dining, food hall, deli/market, and specialist formats were challenged.
- Specialist/broad: marker searches covered pasta, tortillas/mole, dumplings/noodles, hand rolls, tasting menus, sandwiches, and other specialists; absent explicit data remains `unverified`.
- Established/new: OSM `start_date` is sparse; current opening, reopening, relocation, rename, licensing, and 2025–2026 coverage was searched.

## Convergence

A fresh gap pass ran after deduplication across informal/mobile/private formats, counter/lunch-only venues, underrepresented regional cuisines, and outer-suburb recent openings. It added or identity-merged the 16 named leads recorded above. The identical four-query recent-opening pass was then rerun and returned the same result set, yielding **zero new in-scope candidates**. The set is frozen for Phase 4; Phase 7 may reopen it.

This is source convergence, not a complete census.
